This state\\n33:      * also represents groups which use Kafka only for offset commits and have no members.\\n34:      *\\n35:      * action: respond normally to join group from new members\\n36:      *         respond to sync group with UNKNOWN_MEMBER_ID\\n37:      *         respond to heartbeat with UNKNOWN_MEMBER_ID\\n38:      *         respond to leave group with UNKNOWN_MEMBER_ID\\n39:      *         respond to offset commit with UNKNOWN_MEMBER_ID\\n40:      *         allow offset fetch requests\\n41:      * transition: last offsets removed in periodic expiration task => DEAD\\n42:      *             join group from a new member => PREPARING_REBALANCE\\n43:      *             group is removed by partition emigration => DEAD\\n44:      *             group is removed by expiration => DEAD\\n45:      */\\n46:     EMPTY(\\\"Empty\\\"),\\n47: \\n48:     /**\\n49:      * Group is preparing to rebalance.\\n50:      *\\n51:      * action: respond to heartbeats with REBALANCE_IN_PROGRESS\\n52:      *         respond to sync group with REBALANCE_IN_PROGRESS\\n53:      *         remove member on leave group request\\n54:      *         park join group requests from new or existing members until all expected members have joined\\n55:      *         allow offset commits from previous generation\\n56:      *         allow offset fetch requests\\n57:      * transition: some members have joined by the timeout => COMPLETING_REBALANCE\\n58:      *             all members have left the group => EMPTY\\n59:      *             group is removed by partition emigration => DEAD\\n60:      */\\n61:     PREPARING_REBALANCE(\\\"PreparingRebalance\\\"),\\n62: \\n63:     /**\\n64:      * Group is awaiting state assignment from the leader.\\n65:      *\\n66:      * action: respond to heartbeats with REBALANCE_IN_PROGRESS\\n67:      *         respond to offset commits with REBALANCE_IN_PROGRESS\\n68:      *         park sync group requests from followers until transition to STABLE\\n69:      *         allow offset fetch requests\\n70:      * transition: sync group with state assignment received from leader => STABLE\\n71:      *             join group from new member or existing member with updated metadata => PREPARING_REBALANCE\\n72:      *             leave group from existing member => PREPARING_REBALANCE\\n73:      *             member failure detected => PREPARING_REBALANCE\\n74:      *             group is removed by partition emigration => DEAD\\n75:      */\\n76:     COMPLETING_REBALANCE(\\\"CompletingRebalance\\\"),\\n77: \\n78:     /**\\n79:      * Group is stable.\\n80:      *\\n81:      * action: respond to member heartbeats normally\\n82:      *         respond to sync group from any member with current assignment\\n83:      *         respond to join group from followers with matching metadata with current group metadata\\n84:      *         allow offset commits from member of current generation\\n85:      *         allow offset fetch requests\\n86:      * transition: member failure detected via heartbeat => PREPARING_REBALANCE\\n87:      *             leave group from existing member => PREPARING_REBALANCE\\n88:      *             leader join-group received => PREPARING_REBALANCE\\n89:      *             follower join-group with new metadata => PREPARING_REBALANCE\\n90:      *             group is removed by partition emigration => DEAD\\n91:      */\\n92:     STABLE(\\\"Stable\\\"),\\n93: \\n94:     /**\\n95:      * Group has no more members and its metadata is being removed.\\n96:      *\\n97:      * action: respond to join group with UNKNOWN_MEMBER_ID\\n98:      *         respond to sync group with UNKNOWN_MEMBER_ID\\n99:      *         respond to heartbeat with UNKNOWN_MEMBER_ID\\n100:      *         respond to leave group with UNKNOWN_MEMBER_ID\\n101:      *         respond to offset commit with UNKNOWN_MEMBER_ID\\n102:      *         allow offset fetch requests\\n103:      * transition: DEAD is a final state before group metadata is cleaned up, so there are no transitions\\n104:      */\\n105:     DEAD(\\\"Dead\\\");\\n106: \\n107:     private final String name;\\n108:     private The Apache Kafka group coordinator is responsible for managing consumer groups and coordinating rebalancing operations.\\n\\n## State Machines\\n\\nThe repository contains three main state machines for different group types:\\n\\n1. **ClassicGroupState** (sg-evals/kafka--0753c489/group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/classic/ClassicGroupState.java): Defines the state machine for classic consumer groups with five states:\\n   - EMPTY: Group has no members, lingers until offsets expire\\n   - PREPARING_REBALANCE: Group is preparing to rebalance, heartbeats trigger REBALANCE_IN_PROGRESS errors\\n   - COMPLETING_REBALANCE: Group awaits assignment from leader, sync group requests are parked\\n   - STABLE: Group is stable, members send normal heartbeats\\n   - DEAD: Final state before group metadata cleanup\\n\\n2. **ConsumerGroupState** (in sg-evals/kafka--0753c489/group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/modern/consumer/ConsumerGroup.java): States for the modern consumer group protocol:\\n   - The Apache Kafka group coordinator is responsible for managing consumer groups and coordinating rebalancing operations.\\n\\n## State Machines\\n\\nThe repository contains three main state machines for different group types:\\n\\n1. **ClassicGroupState** (sg-evals/kafka--0753c489/group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/classic/ClassicGroupState.java): Defines the state machine for classic consumer groups with five states:\\n   -
